\"RequestMetrics\"}\n  ],\n  \"chain\": [],\n  \"text\": \"Both Kubernetes (v1.32.0) and Grafana (v11.4.0) use the Prometheus client_golang library to implement metrics exposition, but they organize their metrics infrastructure quite differently.\\n\\n## Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)\\n\\n### Core Metrics Infrastructure: k8s.io/component-base/metrics\\n\\nKubernetes builds a **stability-framework wrapper** around the raw Prometheus library, located in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/`.\\n\\n**Registry layer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`):\\n- `KubeRegistry` interface wraps `prometheus.Registerer`/`prometheus.Gatherer` with Kubernetes-specific lifecycle methods (`Register`, `MustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, `RawMustRegister`, `Gather`, `Reset`, `RegisterMetaMetrics`).\\n- `kubeRegistry` struct implements `KubeRegistry`, holding a `PromRegistry` (a `prometheus.Registry`), the binary version (semver), and maps of `hiddenCollectors` and `stableCollectors`.\\n- `NewKubeRegistry()` / `newKubeRegistry()` construct a new instance, appending it to a global `registries` slice so that `SetShowHidden()` can re-register hidden metrics at runtime.\\n- The `Registerable` interface requires `prometheus.Collector` + `Create(version)`, `ClearState()`, and `FQName()` — enabling version-gated metric hiding/deprecation.\\n- `SetShowHidden()`, `SetDisabledMetric()`, `ValidateShowHiddenMetricsVersion()` implement Kubernetes's metric deprecation lifecycle.\\n- Meta-metrics `registeredMetricsTotal`, `disabledMetricsTotal`, `hiddenMetricsTotal` are registered via `RegisterMetaMetrics()`.\\n\\n**Global/legacy registry** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go`):\\n- `defaultRegistry` is the singleton `KubeRegistry` used by nearly all Kubernetes components.\\n- Package-level `MustRegister`, `Register`, `RawMustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, `Registerer`, `DefaultGatherer` functions delegate to `defaultRegistry`.\\n- In `init()`, process and Go runtime collectors (`collectors.NewProcessCollector`, `collectors.NewGoCollector`) are registered, and meta-metrics are initialized.\\n- `Handler()` returns an HTTP handler via `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler(prometheus.DefaultRegisterer, promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...))` — this is the core exposition handler.\\n- `HandlerWithReset()` additionally supports DELETE to reset all metric values.\\n\\n**HTTP exposition** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/http.go`):\\n- `HandlerFor(reg Gatherer, opts HandlerOpts)` wraps `promhttp.HandlerFor` with Kubernetes-specific opts (process start time).\\n- `HandlerWithReset(reg KubeRegistry, opts HandlerOpts)` wraps the handler to call `reg.Reset()` on DELETE requests.\\n\\n**Collector abstraction** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/collector.go`):\\n- `StableCollector` interface extends `prometheus.Collector` with `DescribeWithStability`, `CollectWithStability`, `Create(version, self)`, `ClearState()`, `HiddenMetrics()`.\\n- `BaseStableCollector` provides a base implementation supporting hidden/registerable descriptor tracking per binary version.\\n\\n**Metric type wrappers**: `counter.go` (`Counter`), `gauge.go` (`Gauge`), `histogram.go` (`Histogram`), `summary.go` (`Summary`) all wrap their Prometheus counterparts with a `lazyMetric` pattern (lazy initialization gated on `Create(version)`).\\n\\n**Prometheus exposition endpoint installation**:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`: `DefaultMetrics` and `MetricsWithReset` types install the `/metrics` endpoint on a `mux.PathRecorderMux` via `c.Handle(\\\"/metrics\\\", legacyregistry.Handler())`. The `register()` function triggers registration of apiserver-specific metric collectors (`apimetrics.Register()`, `cachermetrics.Register()`, `etcd3metrics.Register()`, `flowcontrolmetrics.Register()`, `peerproxymetrics.Register()`, `handlersmetrics.Register()`).\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/app/serve.go`: `NewBaseHandler()` adds `mux.Handle(\\\"/metrics\\\", legacyregistry.Handler())` for controller-manager components.\\n- `cmd/kube-proxy/app/server.go` and `cmd/kube-scheduler/app/server.go` similarly call `legacyregistry.Handler()` to install the `/metrics` endpoint.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/server/server.go` wires the kubelet's `/metrics` endpoint.\\n\\n**Sub-packages for domain-specific metrics collectors** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/`):\\n- `workqueue/metrics.go` — registers workqueue metrics\\n- `feature/metrics.go` — feature gate metrics\\n- `slis/metrics.go`, `slis/registry.go`, `slis/routes.go` — SLI/SLO metrics with dedicated HTTP routes\\n- `restclient/metrics.go` — REST client metrics\\n- `clientgo/metrics.go` — client-go metrics aggregator (imports leaderelection, restclient, workqueue)\\n- `controllers/metrics.go`, `meta/metrics.go`, `version/metrics.go` — controller and version metrics\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\nGrafana uses the Prometheus client_golang library more directly, with its own registry provisioning and a dual-gatherer model that combines Kubernetes-style (via `k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry`) and native Prometheus registries.\\n\\n**Core metrics package** (`pkg/infra/metrics/`):\\n\\n- `metrics.go`: Declares `ExporterName = \\\"grafana\\\"` as the Prometheus namespace prefix and defines all global metric variables as bare `prometheus.*` types (e.g., `MInstanceStart prometheus.Counter`, `MPageStatus *prometheus.CounterVec`, `MStatTotalDashboards prometheus.Gauge`, etc.).\\n  - `init()` sets up metric objects with the `grafana` namespace prefix.\\n  - `initMetricVars(reg prometheus.Registerer)` performs bulk registration of all core Grafana metrics via `reg.MustRegister(...)`.\\n\\n- `service.go`: `ProvideService(cfg, reg prometheus.Registerer)` is the wire injection point that calls `initMetricVars(reg)` and `initFrontendMetrics(reg)` to register all metrics.\\n  - `InternalMetricsService` is a background service that also bridges metrics to Graphite via `graphitebridge.NewBridge`.\\n  - `ProvideRegisterer()` returns `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (from Kubernetes's component-base) as the global registerer — meaning Grafana reuses the Kubernetes global registry for metric registration.\\n  - `ProvideGatherer()` constructs a **composite gatherer**: `newMultiRegistry(newAddPrefixWrapper(legacyregistry.DefaultGatherer), prometheus.DefaultGatherer)`. This combines metrics from the Kubernetes-style registry (with a `grafana_` prefix enforcement) and the default Prometheus registry.\\n  - `addPrefixWrapper` ensures all metric names are prefixed with `grafana_` unless they already start with `grafana_` or `go_`.\\n  - `multiRegistry` deduplicates metric names across the two gatherers (allowing `go_*` duplicates).\\n\\n- `frontendmetrics.go`: `initFrontendMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer)` registers frontend-specific histograms (boot time, first paint, etc.) under the `grafana` namespace.\\n\\n- `settings.go`: `readSettings()` configures the Graphite bridge interval and address; `parseGraphiteSettings()` populates a `graphitebridge.Config` using `prometheus.DefaultGatherer` for the bridge source.\\n\\n- `metricutil/utils.go`: Helper functions `NewCounterStartingAtZero` and `NewCounterVecStartingAtZero` initialize counters with a zero observation to guarantee metric time-series existence from startup.\\n\\n**HTTP /metrics endpoint exposition**:\\n- `pkg/server/instrumentation_service.go`: `instrumentationService` / `NewInstrumentationService` creates a standalone HTTP server with `newInstrumentationServer()`, which registers `promhttp.Handler()` (using Prometheus's default gatherer) on `/metrics`. This provides an instrumentation-only endpoint on a separate port.\\n- `pkg/api/http_server.go`: The main Grafana HTTP server (`HTTPServer`) also serves `/metrics` by calling `promhttp.HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true})` — using the composite `promGatherer` (which combines the Kubernetes legacy registry with the Prometheus default registry). This endpoint supports OpenMetrics format and optional basic authentication.\\n\\n**Request-level metrics middleware** (`pkg/middleware/request_metrics.go`): `RequestMetrics` is a web middleware that instruments HTTP requests with `http_request_in_flight` gauge and `http_request_duration_seconds` histogram, registered directly against the injected `prometheus.Registerer`.\\n\\n**Subsystem-specific metric collectors** (each subsystem creates its own scoped registry/sub-namespace):\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/` — alerting subsystem (scheduler, alertmanager, API, historian, state, multi-org, remote alertmanager, remote writer)\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/metrics.go`, `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/metrics.go`, `pkg/services/auth/idimpl/metrics.go` — auth subsystem metrics\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/service/metrics.go`, `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/metrics.go` — storage metrics\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go` — HTTP client metrics\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Comparison\\n\\n| Aspect | Kubernetes | Grafana |\\n|---|---|---|  \\n| **Registry** | Custom `KubeRegistry` wrapping `prometheus.Registry`; global singleton in `legacyregistry.defaultRegistry` | Injects `prometheus.Registerer` (backed by k8s `legacyregistry.Registerer()`); composite gatherer combining two registries |\\n| **Collector abstraction** | `Registerable` + `StableCollector` / `BaseStableCollector` for version-gated metric hiding | Direct `prometheus.Collector` types; no versioned lifecycle |\\n| **Metric types** | Custom wrappers (`Counter`, `Gauge`, `Histogram`, `Summary`) with lazy initialization and stability levels | Native `prometheus.*` types directly |\\n| **/metrics endpoint** | `legacyregistry.Handler()` → `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...)` installed via `DefaultMetrics.Install()` or `mux.Handle()` in each component | `promhttp.HandlerFor(compositeGatherer, ...)` in `HTTPServer`; separate `instrumentationService` with `promhttp.Handler()` |\\n| **OpenMetrics** | Not explicitly enabled | Enabled via `HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true}` |\\n| **Extra exposition** | DELETE method on `/metrics` resets counters (`HandlerWithReset`) | Optional basic auth on `/metrics` endpoint |\\n| **Metric naming** | Namespaced by subsystem (no global prefix enforcement) | `grafana_` namespace prefix enforced by `addPrefixWrapper` on the k8s legacy gatherer |\\n| **Side-channel export** | Not built-in | Graphite bridge (`graphitebridge`) for pushing metrics |\\n| **Subsystem organization** | Many per-package `metrics.go` files, each calling `legacyregistry.MustRegister` in a `Register()` function or `init()` | Per-subsystem `metrics.go` files that take `prometheus.Registerer` as a constructor argument |\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2746,"cache_read_input_tokens":59022,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":2746,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"25af3920-877f-49e0-9f4b-c9cf099efc85","uuid":"a79d0392-0a69-4bc4-96e7-8680277983e0"}

\"RequestMetrics\"}\n  ],\n  \"chain\": [],\n  \"text\": \"Both Kubernetes (v1.32.0) and Grafana (v11.4.0) use the Prometheus client_golang library to implement metrics exposition, but they organize their metrics infrastructure quite differently.\\n\\n## Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)\\n\\n### Core Metrics Infrastructure: k8s.io/component-base/metrics\\n\\nKubernetes builds a **stability-framework wrapper** around the raw Prometheus library, located in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/`.\\n\\n**Registry layer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`):\\n- `KubeRegistry` interface wraps `prometheus.Registerer`/`prometheus.Gatherer` with Kubernetes-specific lifecycle methods (`Register`, `MustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, `RawMustRegister`, `Gather`, `Reset`, `RegisterMetaMetrics`).\\n- `kubeRegistry` struct implements `KubeRegistry`, holding a `PromRegistry` (a `prometheus.Registry`), the binary version (semver), and maps of `hiddenCollectors` and `stableCollectors`.\\n- `NewKubeRegistry()` / `newKubeRegistry()` construct a new instance, appending it to a global `registries` slice so that `SetShowHidden()` can re-register hidden metrics at runtime.\\n- The `Registerable` interface requires `prometheus.Collector` + `Create(version)`, `ClearState()`, and `FQName()` — enabling version-gated metric hiding/deprecation.\\n- `SetShowHidden()`, `SetDisabledMetric()`, `ValidateShowHiddenMetricsVersion()` implement Kubernetes's metric deprecation lifecycle.\\n- Meta-metrics `registeredMetricsTotal`, `disabledMetricsTotal`, `hiddenMetricsTotal` are registered via `RegisterMetaMetrics()`.\\n\\n**Global/legacy registry** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go`):\\n- `defaultRegistry` is the singleton `KubeRegistry` used by nearly all Kubernetes components.\\n- Package-level `MustRegister`, `Register`, `RawMustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, `Registerer`, `DefaultGatherer` functions delegate to `defaultRegistry`.\\n- In `init()`, process and Go runtime collectors (`collectors.NewProcessCollector`, `collectors.NewGoCollector`) are registered, and meta-metrics are initialized.\\n- `Handler()` returns an HTTP handler via `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler(prometheus.DefaultRegisterer, promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...))` — this is the core exposition handler.\\n- `HandlerWithReset()` additionally supports DELETE to reset all metric values.\\n\\n**HTTP exposition** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/http.go`):\\n- `HandlerFor(reg Gatherer, opts HandlerOpts)` wraps `promhttp.HandlerFor` with Kubernetes-specific opts (process start time).\\n- `HandlerWithReset(reg KubeRegistry, opts HandlerOpts)` wraps the handler to call `reg.Reset()` on DELETE requests.\\n\\n**Collector abstraction** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/collector.go`):\\n- `StableCollector` interface extends `prometheus.Collector` with `DescribeWithStability`, `CollectWithStability`, `Create(version, self)`, `ClearState()`, `HiddenMetrics()`.\\n- `BaseStableCollector` provides a base implementation supporting hidden/registerable descriptor tracking per binary version.\\n\\n**Metric type wrappers**: `counter.go` (`Counter`), `gauge.go` (`Gauge`), `histogram.go` (`Histogram`), `summary.go` (`Summary`) all wrap their Prometheus counterparts with a `lazyMetric` pattern (lazy initialization gated on `Create(version)`).\\n\\n**Prometheus exposition endpoint installation**:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`: `DefaultMetrics` and `MetricsWithReset` types install the `/metrics` endpoint on a `mux.PathRecorderMux` via `c.Handle(\\\"/metrics\\\", legacyregistry.Handler())`. The `register()` function triggers registration of apiserver-specific metric collectors (`apimetrics.Register()`, `cachermetrics.Register()`, `etcd3metrics.Register()`, `flowcontrolmetrics.Register()`, `peerproxymetrics.Register()`, `handlersmetrics.Register()`).\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/app/serve.go`: `NewBaseHandler()` adds `mux.Handle(\\\"/metrics\\\", legacyregistry.Handler())` for controller-manager components.\\n- `cmd/kube-proxy/app/server.go` and `cmd/kube-scheduler/app/server.go` similarly call `legacyregistry.Handler()` to install the `/metrics` endpoint.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/server/server.go` wires the kubelet's `/metrics` endpoint.\\n\\n**Sub-packages for domain-specific metrics collectors** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/`):\\n- `workqueue/metrics.go` — registers workqueue metrics\\n- `feature/metrics.go` — feature gate metrics\\n- `slis/metrics.go`, `slis/registry.go`, `slis/routes.go` — SLI/SLO metrics with dedicated HTTP routes\\n- `restclient/metrics.go` — REST client metrics\\n- `clientgo/metrics.go` — client-go metrics aggregator (imports leaderelection, restclient, workqueue)\\n- `controllers/metrics.go`, `meta/metrics.go`, `version/metrics.go` — controller and version metrics\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\nGrafana uses the Prometheus client_golang library more directly, with its own registry provisioning and a dual-gatherer model that combines Kubernetes-style (via `k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry`) and native Prometheus registries.\\n\\n**Core metrics package** (`pkg/infra/metrics/`):\\n\\n- `metrics.go`: Declares `ExporterName = \\\"grafana\\\"` as the Prometheus namespace prefix and defines all global metric variables as bare `prometheus.*` types (e.g., `MInstanceStart prometheus.Counter`, `MPageStatus *prometheus.CounterVec`, `MStatTotalDashboards prometheus.Gauge`, etc.).\\n  - `init()` sets up metric objects with the `grafana` namespace prefix.\\n  - `initMetricVars(reg prometheus.Registerer)` performs bulk registration of all core Grafana metrics via `reg.MustRegister(...)`.\\n\\n- `service.go`: `ProvideService(cfg, reg prometheus.Registerer)` is the wire injection point that calls `initMetricVars(reg)` and `initFrontendMetrics(reg)` to register all metrics.\\n  - `InternalMetricsService` is a background service that also bridges metrics to Graphite via `graphitebridge.NewBridge`.\\n  - `ProvideRegisterer()` returns `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (from Kubernetes's component-base) as the global registerer — meaning Grafana reuses the Kubernetes global registry for metric registration.\\n  - `ProvideGatherer()` constructs a **composite gatherer**: `newMultiRegistry(newAddPrefixWrapper(legacyregistry.DefaultGatherer), prometheus.DefaultGatherer)`. This combines metrics from the Kubernetes-style registry (with a `grafana_` prefix enforcement) and the default Prometheus registry.\\n  - `addPrefixWrapper` ensures all metric names are prefixed with `grafana_` unless they already start with `grafana_` or `go_`.\\n  - `multiRegistry` deduplicates metric names across the two gatherers (allowing `go_*` duplicates).\\n\\n- `frontendmetrics.go`: `initFrontendMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer)` registers frontend-specific histograms (boot time, first paint, etc.) under the `grafana` namespace.\\n\\n- `settings.go`: `readSettings()` configures the Graphite bridge interval and address; `parseGraphiteSettings()` populates a `graphitebridge.Config` using `prometheus.DefaultGatherer` for the bridge source.\\n\\n- `metricutil/utils.go`: Helper functions `NewCounterStartingAtZero` and `NewCounterVecStartingAtZero` initialize counters with a zero observation to guarantee metric time-series existence from startup.\\n\\n**HTTP /metrics endpoint exposition**:\\n- `pkg/server/instrumentation_service.go`: `instrumentationService` / `NewInstrumentationService` creates a standalone HTTP server with `newInstrumentationServer()`, which registers `promhttp.Handler()` (using Prometheus's default gatherer) on `/metrics`. This provides an instrumentation-only endpoint on a separate port.\\n- `pkg/api/http_server.go`: The main Grafana HTTP server (`HTTPServer`) also serves `/metrics` by calling `promhttp.HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true})` — using the composite `promGatherer` (which combines the Kubernetes legacy registry with the Prometheus default registry). This endpoint supports OpenMetrics format and optional basic authentication.\\n\\n**Request-level metrics middleware** (`pkg/middleware/request_metrics.go`): `RequestMetrics` is a web middleware that instruments HTTP requests with `http_request_in_flight` gauge and `http_request_duration_seconds` histogram, registered directly against the injected `prometheus.Registerer`.\\n\\n**Subsystem-specific metric collectors** (each subsystem creates its own scoped registry/sub-namespace):\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/` — alerting subsystem (scheduler, alertmanager, API, historian, state, multi-org, remote alertmanager, remote writer)\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/metrics.go`, `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/metrics.go`, `pkg/services/auth/idimpl/metrics.go` — auth subsystem metrics\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/service/metrics.go`, `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/metrics.go` — storage metrics\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go` — HTTP client metrics\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Comparison\\n\\n| Aspect | Kubernetes | Grafana |\\n|---|---|---|  \\n| **Registry** | Custom `KubeRegistry` wrapping `prometheus.Registry`; global singleton in `legacyregistry.defaultRegistry` | Injects `prometheus.Registerer` (backed by k8s `legacyregistry.Registerer()`); composite gatherer combining two registries |\\n| **Collector abstraction** | `Registerable` + `StableCollector` / `BaseStableCollector` for version-gated metric hiding | Direct `prometheus.Collector` types; no versioned lifecycle |\\n| **Metric types** | Custom wrappers (`Counter`, `Gauge`, `Histogram`, `Summary`) with lazy initialization and stability levels | Native `prometheus.*` types directly |\\n| **/metrics endpoint** | `legacyregistry.Handler()` → `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...)` installed via `DefaultMetrics.Install()` or `mux.Handle()` in each component | `promhttp.HandlerFor(compositeGatherer, ...)` in `HTTPServer`; The global singleton `defaultRegistry` lives in `legacyregistry/registry.go`.\n- `legacyregistry/registry.go`: Package-level `MustRegister`, `Register`, `Handler()`, `HandlerWithReset()` functions delegate to `defaultRegistry`. `Handler()` wraps `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...)`.\n- `http.go`: `HandlerFor` / `HandlerWithReset` wrap `promhttp` handlers.\n- `collector.go`: `StableCollector` / `BaseStableCollector` enable version-gated hiding of metrics.\n- **`/metrics` endpoint**: Installed by `DefaultMetrics.Install()` or `MetricsWithReset.Install()` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`, calling `legacyregistry.Handler()`. Also wired in `controller-manager/app/serve.go`, `cmd/kube-proxy`, `cmd/kube-scheduler`, `pkg/kubelet/server/server.go`.\n\n## Grafana Metrics Exposition Pattern\n\n**Core infrastructure** in `pkg/infra/metrics/`:\n- `metrics.go`: Global metric variables (counters, gauges, histograms) declared as bare `prometheus.*` types, registered in bulk by `initMetricVars(reg)`.\n- `service.go`: `ProvideRegisterer()` returns the Kubernetes `legacyregistry.Registerer()`; `ProvideGatherer()` returns a **composite gatherer** combining `addPrefixWrapper(legacyregistry.DefaultGatherer)` + `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`. The `addPrefixWrapper` enforces `grafana_` prefix on all metric names.\n- **`/metrics` endpoint**: Served two ways — `pkg/server/instrumentation_service.go` (`instrumentationService`) runs a dedicated HTTP server using `promhttp.Handler()`, while `pkg/api/http_server.go` serves the same path via `promhttp.HandlerFor(compositeGatherer, HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true})` with optional basic auth."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":7820,"cache_read_input_tokens":61768,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":7820,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"25af3920-877f-49e0-9f4b-c9cf099efc85","uuid":"a217d382-33a4-4d2d-901c-b0a0b3c94c23"}
